# <a name="required-mobile-diagnostic-data-for-microsoft-teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="efca4-103">Microsoft Teams 適用的行動裝置必要診斷資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-103">Required mobile diagnostic data for Microsoft Teams</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="efca4-104">下列文章包含 Microsoft Teams 行動裝置事件的清單，以及每個事件收集的屬性清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-104">The following article contains a list of Microsoft Teams mobile events, and lists of properties each event collects.</span></span>

## <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="efca4-105">事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-105">Events</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="efca4-106">以下所列的所有事件有共同的屬性，若要檢閱這些屬性，請參閱[隨著所有事件傳送的屬性](#properties-sent-with-all-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-106">There are common properties for all events listed below, to review them, see [Properties sent with all events](#properties-sent-with-all-events).</span></span>

### <a name="panelaction"></a><span data-ttu-id="efca4-107">PanelAction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-107">PanelAction</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="efca4-108">如需 PanelAction事件屬性的詳細資訊，請參閱[隨著面板動作事件傳送的屬性](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-108">For information on the properties of PanelAction events, see [Properties sent with panelaction events](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - 當使用者切換協助工具功能時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - When a users toggles an accessibility feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - 確認 [我們已更新通知設定] 對話方塊中的更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - Acknowledge an update in the we updated a notification setting dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efca4-111">這是用來確認更新通知並決定整體通知可靠性的功能成功度量值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-111">This is a feature success metrics used to acknowledge update notifications and to determine overall notification reliability.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="efca4-113">建立訊息擴充使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-113">Create message extension usage.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="efca4-114">操作訊息擴充使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-114">Action message extension usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - 已關閉共用作用中提醒的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - The location sharing active reminder banner was dismissed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-116">**activityChatClicked** - 當系統選取 **[活動]** 索引標籤中的 [非即時聊天]，或顯示出分割視圖時，進行觸發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-116">**activityChatClicked** - Triggered when non-live chat is selected in the **Activity** tab or a split view is shown.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-117">\*\*activityCoNtextMenu \*\* - 活動摘要中的溢出動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-117">**activityContextMenu** - Overflow actions in the activity feed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-118">**activityFeedClick** - 已點選活動摘要專案，並導至聊天機器人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-118">**activityFeedClick** - An activity feed item is tapped on and a bot chat is navigated to.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - 在摘要專案上擷取長按手勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - Captures long press gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - 在摘要專案上擷取滑動手勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - Captures swipe gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-121">**activityFilterClick** - 擷取活動篩選使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-121">**activityFilterClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - 擷取活動篩選使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - 擷取活動篩選使用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** -當系統選取 **[活動]** 索引標籤上的 [即時會議] 中的 [聊天] 時，進行觸發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - Triggered when chat is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - 當系統選取 **[活動]** 索引標籤上的 [即時會議] 中的 **[詳細資料]** 時，觸發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - Triggered when **Details** is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-126">**activityTabClicked** -可協助您判斷：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-126">**activityTabClicked** - Helps to determine if:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="efca4-127">**[活動]** 索引標籤已顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-127">The **Activity** tab is shown.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="efca4-128">小組會擷取 **[事件]** 索引標籤事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-128">Teams captures an **Activity** tab event.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-129">**activityTypeDropdown** -擷取活動篩選使用情況，以在 **[我的活動]** 和 **[摘要]** 之間進行切換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - Captures activity filter usage to switch between **My Activity** and **Feeds**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-130">**addChannel** - 新增頻道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-130">**addChannel** - Adding a channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efca4-131">這個專案提供成功建立頻道的成功資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-131">This item provides success data around the successful creation of a channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-132">**addMember** - 已觸發選取 **[更多]** 功能表中的 **[邀請人員]** 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-132">**addMember** - Triggered the **Invite people** button is selected in the **More** menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-133">**addMembers** - 新增成員至小組或私人頻道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-133">**addMembers** - Add members to a team or private channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-134">**addToCalendar** - 針對私人行事曆中遺失的行事曆事件，選取 **新增至行事曆** 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-134">**addToCalendar** - Select the **Add to calendar** button for calendar events missing in private calendar.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-136">**addToMeeting** - 選取會議參與者清單中的 **[新增至會議]** 按鈕 (適用于交談中的參與者)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-136">**addToMeeting** - Select the **Add to meeting** button in the participant list for a meeting (for participants who are a part of the chat).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-138">**admitAll** -從 [會議廳] 區段中選取 **[允許所有]** 按鈕的次數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-138">**admitAll** - The number of times the **Admit all** button is selected from the lobby section.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="efca4-141">**android：null** - 將聊天機器人設為靜音或取消靜音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-141">**android: null** - Mute or unmute a bot chat.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="efca4-142">這會加強聊天中現有的遙測，只會增加應用程式資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-142">This is enhancing existing telemetry around chats only adds application information.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="efca4-1466">屬性名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-1466">Property name</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="efca4-1467">說明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-1467">Description</span></span> |
|----------------------|-------------|

| <span data-ttu-id="efca4-1470">Scenario_Step</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-1470">Scenario_Step</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="efca4-1471">當案例包含多個具有不同失敗點的步驟時，此屬性會擷取該步驟的詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-1471">When a scenario contains multiple steps with different failure points, this property captures details about the step</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="efca4-1472">Scenario_StatusCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-1472">Scenario_StatusCode</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="efca4-1473">屬性根據案例成功或失敗來記錄案例的狀態代碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="efca4-1473">Property records status code of the scenario based on scenario success or failure</span></span> |
